80#ifdef __POSIX__1
81constexpr char kPathSeparator = '/';
82#else
83const char* const kPathSeparator = "\\/";
84#endif
85
86std::string Basename(const std::string& str, const std::string& extension) {
87 // Remove everything leading up to and including the final path separator.
88 std::string::size_type pos = str.find_last_of(kPathSeparator);
89
90 // Starting index for the resulting string
91 std::size_t start_pos = 0;
92 // String size to return
93 std::size_t str_size = str.size();
94 if (pos != std::string::npos) {
95 start_pos = pos + 1;
96 str_size -= start_pos;
97 }
98
99 // Strip away the extension, if any.
100 if (str_size >= extension.size() &&
101 str.compare(str.size() - extension.size(),
102 extension.size(), extension) == 0) {
103 str_size -= extension.size();
104 }
105
106 return str.substr(start_pos, str_size);
107}

144// The FileHandle object wraps a file descriptor and will close it on garbage
145// collection if necessary. If that happens, a process warning will be
146// emitted (or a fatal exception will occur if the fd cannot be closed.)
147FileHandle::FileHandle(BindingData* binding_data,
148 Local<Object> obj, int fd)
149 : AsyncWrap(binding_data->env(), obj, AsyncWrap::PROVIDER_FILEHANDLE),
150 StreamBase(env()),
151 fd_(fd),
152 binding_data_(binding_data) {
153 MakeWeak();
154 StreamBase::AttachToObject(GetObject());
155}
156
157FileHandle* FileHandle::New(BindingData* binding_data,
158 int fd, Local<Object> obj) {
159 Environment* env = binding_data->env();
160 if (obj.IsEmpty() && !env->fd_constructor_template()
161 ->NewInstance(env->context())
162 .ToLocal(&obj)) {
163 return nullptr;
164 }
165 return new FileHandle(binding_data, obj, fd);
166}

200FileHandle::TransferMode FileHandle::GetTransferMode() const {
201 return reading_ || closing_ || closed_ ?
202 TransferMode::kUntransferable : TransferMode::kTransferable;
203}

222BaseObjectPtr<BaseObject> FileHandle::TransferData::Deserialize(
223 Environment* env,
224 v8::Local<v8::Context> context,
225 std::unique_ptr<worker::TransferData> self) {
226 BindingData* bd = Environment::GetBindingData<BindingData>(context);
227 if (bd == nullptr) return {};
228
229 int fd = fd_;
230 fd_ = -1;
231 return BaseObjectPtr<BaseObject> { FileHandle::New(bd, fd) };
232}
233
234// Close the file descriptor if it hasn't already been closed. A process
235// warning will be emitted using a SetImmediate to avoid calling back to
236// JS during GC. If closing the fd fails at this point, a fatal exception
237// will crash the process immediately.
238inline void FileHandle::Close() {
239 if (closed_) return;
240 uv_fs_t req;
241 int ret = uv_fs_close(env()->event_loop(), &req, fd_, nullptr);
242 uv_fs_req_cleanup(&req);
243
244 struct err_detail { int ret; int fd; };
245
246 err_detail detail { ret, fd_ };
247
248 AfterClose();
249
250 if (ret < 0) {
251 // Do not unref this
252 env()->SetImmediate([detail](Environment* env) {
253 char msg[70];
254 snprintf(msg, arraysize(msg),
255 "Closing file descriptor %d on garbage collection failed",
256 detail.fd);
257 // This exception will end up being fatal for the process because
258 // it is being thrown from within the SetImmediate handler and
259 // there is no JS stack to bubble it to. In other words, tearing
260 // down the process is the only reasonable thing we can do here.
261 HandleScope handle_scope(env->isolate());
262 env->ThrowUVException(detail.ret, "close", msg);
263 });
264 return;
265 }
266
267 // If the close was successful, we still want to emit a process warning
268 // to notify that the file descriptor was gc'd. We want to be noisy about
269 // this because not explicitly closing the FileHandle is a bug.
270
271 env()->SetImmediate([detail](Environment* env) {
272 ProcessEmitWarning(env,
273 "Closing file descriptor %d on garbage collection",
274 detail.fd);
275 if (env->filehandle_close_warning()) {
276 env->set_filehandle_close_warning(false);
277 ProcessEmitDeprecationWarning(
278 env,
279 "Closing a FileHandle object on garbage collection is deprecated. "
280 "Please close FileHandle objects explicitly using "
281 "FileHandle.prototype.close(). In the future, an error will be "
282 "thrown if a file descriptor is closed during garbage collection.",
283 "DEP0137").IsNothing();
284 }
285 }, CallbackFlags::kUnrefed);
286}
287
288void FileHandle::CloseReq::Resolve() {
289 Isolate* isolate = env()->isolate();
290 HandleScope scope(isolate);
291 InternalCallbackScope callback_scope(this);
292 Local<Promise> promise = promise_.Get(isolate);
293 Local<Promise::Resolver> resolver = promise.As<Promise::Resolver>();
294 resolver->Resolve(env()->context(), Undefined(isolate)).Check();
295}
296
297void FileHandle::CloseReq::Reject(Local<Value> reason) {
298 Isolate* isolate = env()->isolate();
299 HandleScope scope(isolate);
300 InternalCallbackScope callback_scope(this);
301 Local<Promise> promise = promise_.Get(isolate);
302 Local<Promise::Resolver> resolver = promise.As<Promise::Resolver>();
303 resolver->Reject(env()->context(), reason).Check();
304}
305
306FileHandle* FileHandle::CloseReq::file_handle() {
307 Isolate* isolate = env()->isolate();
308 HandleScope scope(isolate);
309 Local<Value> val = ref_.Get(isolate);
310 Local<Object> obj = val.As<Object>();
311 return Unwrap<FileHandle>(obj);
312}
313
314FileHandle::CloseReq::CloseReq(Environment* env,
315 Local<Object> obj,
316 Local<Promise> promise,
317 Local<Value> ref)
318 : ReqWrap(env, obj, AsyncWrap::PROVIDER_FILEHANDLECLOSEREQ) {
319 promise_.Reset(env->isolate(), promise);
320 ref_.Reset(env->isolate(), ref);
321}
322
323FileHandle::CloseReq::~CloseReq() {
324 uv_fs_req_cleanup(req());
325 promise_.Reset();
326 ref_.Reset();
327}

329void FileHandle::CloseReq::MemoryInfo(MemoryTracker* tracker) const {
330 tracker->TrackField("promise", promise_);

336// Closes this FileHandle asynchronously and returns a Promise that will be
337// resolved when the callback is invoked, or rejects with a UVException if
338// there was a problem closing the fd. This is the preferred mechanism for
339// closing the FD object even tho the object will attempt to close
340// automatically on gc.
341MaybeLocal<Promise> FileHandle::ClosePromise() {
342 Isolate* isolate = env()->isolate();
343 EscapableHandleScope scope(isolate);
344 Local<Context> context = env()->context();
345 auto maybe_resolver = Promise::Resolver::New(context);
346 CHECK(!maybe_resolver.IsEmpty())do { if (__builtin_expect(!!(!(!maybe_resolver.IsEmpty())), 0
)) { do { static const node::AssertionInfo args = { "../src/node_file.cc"
":" "346", "!maybe_resolver.IsEmpty()", __PRETTY_FUNCTION__ }
; node::Assert(args); } while (0); } } while (0);
347 Local<Promise::Resolver> resolver = maybe_resolver.ToLocalChecked();
348 Local<Promise> promise = resolver.As<Promise>();
349 CHECK(!reading_)do { if (__builtin_expect(!!(!(!reading_)), 0)) { do { static
const node::AssertionInfo args = { "../src/node_file.cc" ":"
"349", "!reading_", __PRETTY_FUNCTION__ }; node::Assert(args
); } while (0); } } while (0);
350 if (!closed_ && !closing_) {
351 closing_ = true;
352 Local<Object> close_req_obj;
353 if (!env()
354 ->fdclose_constructor_template()
355 ->NewInstance(env()->context())
356 .ToLocal(&close_req_obj)) {
357 return MaybeLocal<Promise>();
358 }
359 CloseReq* req = new CloseReq(env(), close_req_obj, promise, object());
360 auto AfterClose = uv_fs_callback_t{[](uv_fs_t* req) {
361 std::unique_ptr<CloseReq> close(CloseReq::from_req(req));
362 CHECK_NOT_NULL(close)do { if (__builtin_expect(!!(!((close) != nullptr)), 0)) { do
{ static const node::AssertionInfo args = { "../src/node_file.cc"
":" "362", "(close) != nullptr", __PRETTY_FUNCTION__ }; node
::Assert(args); } while (0); } } while (0);
363 close->file_handle()->AfterClose();
364 Isolate* isolate = close->env()->isolate();
365 if (req->result < 0) {
366 HandleScope handle_scope(isolate);
367 close->Reject(UVException(isolate, req->result, "close"));
368 } else {
369 close->Resolve();
370 }
371 }};
372 int ret = req->Dispatch(uv_fs_close, fd_, AfterClose);
373 if (ret < 0) {
374 req->Reject(UVException(isolate, ret, "close"));
375 delete req;
376 }
377 } else {
378 // Already closed. Just reject the promise immediately
379 resolver->Reject(context, UVException(isolate, UV_EBADF, "close"))
380 .Check();
381 }
382 return scope.Escape(promise);
383}
384
385void FileHandle::Close(const FunctionCallbackInfo<Value>& args) {
386 FileHandle* fd;
387 ASSIGN_OR_RETURN_UNWRAP(&fd, args.Holder())do { *&fd = static_cast<typename std::remove_reference
<decltype(*&fd)>::type>( BaseObject::FromJSObject
(args.Holder())); if (*&fd == nullptr) return ; } while (
0);
388 Local<Promise> ret;
389 if (!fd->ClosePromise().ToLocal(&ret)) return;
390 args.GetReturnValue().Set(ret);
391}
392
393
394void FileHandle::ReleaseFD(const FunctionCallbackInfo<Value>& args) {
395 FileHandle* fd;
396 ASSIGN_OR_RETURN_UNWRAP(&fd, args.Holder())do { *&fd = static_cast<typename std::remove_reference
<decltype(*&fd)>::type>( BaseObject::FromJSObject
(args.Holder())); if (*&fd == nullptr) return ; } while (
0);
397 // Just act as if this FileHandle has been closed.
398 fd->AfterClose();
399}
400
401
402void FileHandle::AfterClose() {
403 closing_ = false;
404 closed_ = true;
405 fd_ = -1;
406 if (reading_ && !persistent().IsEmpty())
407 EmitRead(UV_EOF);
408}
409
410void FileHandleReadWrap::MemoryInfo(MemoryTracker* tracker) const {
411 tracker->TrackField("buffer", buffer_);
412 tracker->TrackField("file_handle", this->file_handle_);
413}
414
415FileHandleReadWrap::FileHandleReadWrap(FileHandle* handle, Local<Object> obj)
416 : ReqWrap(handle->env(), obj, AsyncWrap::PROVIDER_FSREQCALLBACK),
417 file_handle_(handle) {}
418
419int FileHandle::ReadStart() {
420 if (!IsAlive() || IsClosing())
421 return UV_EOF;
422
423 reading_ = true;
424
425 if (current_read_)
426 return 0;
427
428 BaseObjectPtr<FileHandleReadWrap> read_wrap;
429
430 if (read_length_ == 0) {
431 EmitRead(UV_EOF);
432 return 0;
433 }
434
435 {
436 // Create a new FileHandleReadWrap or re-use one.
437 // Either way, we need these two scopes for AsyncReset() or otherwise
438 // for creating the new instance.
439 HandleScope handle_scope(env()->isolate());
440 AsyncHooks::DefaultTriggerAsyncIdScope trigger_scope(this);
441
442 auto& freelist = binding_data_->file_handle_read_wrap_freelist;
443 if (freelist.size() > 0) {
444 read_wrap = std::move(freelist.back());
445 freelist.pop_back();
446 // Use a fresh async resource.
447 // Lifetime is ensured via AsyncWrap::resource_.
448 Local<Object> resource = Object::New(env()->isolate());
449 USE(resource->Set(
450 env()->context(), env()->handle_string(), read_wrap->object()));
451 read_wrap->AsyncReset(resource);
452 read_wrap->file_handle_ = this;
453 } else {
454 Local<Object> wrap_obj;
455 if (!env()
456 ->filehandlereadwrap_template()
457 ->NewInstance(env()->context())
458 .ToLocal(&wrap_obj)) {
459 return UV_EBUSY;
460 }
461 read_wrap = MakeDetachedBaseObject<FileHandleReadWrap>(this, wrap_obj);
462 }
463 }
464 int64_t recommended_read = 65536;
465 if (read_length_ >= 0 && read_length_ <= recommended_read)
466 recommended_read = read_length_;
467
468 read_wrap->buffer_ = EmitAlloc(recommended_read);
469
470 current_read_ = std::move(read_wrap);
471
472 current_read_->Dispatch(uv_fs_read,
473 fd_,
474 &current_read_->buffer_,
475 1,
476 read_offset_,
477 uv_fs_callback_t{[](uv_fs_t* req) {
478 FileHandle* handle;
479 {
480 FileHandleReadWrap* req_wrap = FileHandleReadWrap::from_req(req);
481 handle = req_wrap->file_handle_;
482 CHECK_EQ(handle->current_read_.get(), req_wrap)do { if (__builtin_expect(!!(!((handle->current_read_.get(
)) == (req_wrap))), 0)) { do { static const node::AssertionInfo
args = { "../src/node_file.cc" ":" "482", "(handle->current_read_.get()) == (req_wrap)"
, __PRETTY_FUNCTION__ }; node::Assert(args); } while (0); } }
while (0);
483 }
484
485 // ReadStart() checks whether current_read_ is set to determine whether
486 // a read is in progress. Moving it into a local variable makes sure that
487 // the ReadStart() call below doesn't think we're still actively reading.
488 BaseObjectPtr<FileHandleReadWrap> read_wrap =
489 std::move(handle->current_read_);
490
491 int result = req->result;
492 uv_buf_t buffer = read_wrap->buffer_;
493
494 uv_fs_req_cleanup(req);
495
496 // Push the read wrap back to the freelist, or let it be destroyed
497 // once we’re exiting the current scope.
498 constexpr size_t kWantedFreelistFill = 100;
499 auto& freelist = handle->binding_data_->file_handle_read_wrap_freelist;
500 if (freelist.size() < kWantedFreelistFill) {
501 read_wrap->Reset();
502 freelist.emplace_back(std::move(read_wrap));
503 }
504
505 if (result >= 0) {
506 // Read at most as many bytes as we originally planned to.
507 if (handle->read_length_ >= 0 && handle->read_length_ < result)
508 result = handle->read_length_;
509
510 // If we read data and we have an expected length, decrease it by
511 // how much we have read.
512 if (handle->read_length_ >= 0)
513 handle->read_length_ -= result;
514
515 // If we have an offset, increase it by how much we have read.
516 if (handle->read_offset_ >= 0)
517 handle->read_offset_ += result;
518 }
519
520 // Reading 0 bytes from a file always means EOF, or that we reached
521 // the end of the requested range.
522 if (result == 0)
523 result = UV_EOF;
524
525 handle->EmitRead(result, buffer);
526
527 // Start over, if EmitRead() didn’t tell us to stop.
528 if (handle->reading_)
529 handle->ReadStart();
530 }});
531
532 return 0;
533}
534
535int FileHandle::ReadStop() {
536 reading_ = false;
537 return 0;
538}
539
540typedef SimpleShutdownWrap<ReqWrap<uv_fs_t>> FileHandleCloseWrap;
541
542ShutdownWrap* FileHandle::CreateShutdownWrap(Local<Object> object) {
543 return new FileHandleCloseWrap(this, object);
544}
545
546int FileHandle::DoShutdown(ShutdownWrap* req_wrap) {
547 FileHandleCloseWrap* wrap = static_cast<FileHandleCloseWrap*>(req_wrap);
548 closing_ = true;
549 wrap->Dispatch(uv_fs_close, fd_, uv_fs_callback_t{[](uv_fs_t* req) {
550 FileHandleCloseWrap* wrap = static_cast<FileHandleCloseWrap*>(
551 FileHandleCloseWrap::from_req(req));
552 FileHandle* handle = static_cast<FileHandle*>(wrap->stream());
553 handle->AfterClose();
554
555 int result = req->result;
556 uv_fs_req_cleanup(req);
557 wrap->Done(result);
558 }});
559
560 return 0;
561}

564void FSReqCallback::Reject(Local<Value> reject) {
565 MakeCallback(env()->oncomplete_string(), 1, &reject);
566}
567
568void FSReqCallback::ResolveStat(const uv_stat_t* stat) {
569 Resolve(FillGlobalStatsArray(binding_data(), use_bigint(), stat));
570}
571
572void FSReqCallback::Resolve(Local<Value> value) {
573 Local<Value> argv[2] {
574 Null(env()->isolate()),
575 value
576 };
577 MakeCallback(env()->oncomplete_string(),
578 value->IsUndefined() ? 1 : arraysize(argv),
579 argv);
580}

583 args.GetReturnValue().SetUndefined();
584}

586void NewFSReqCallback(const FunctionCallbackInfo<Value>& args) {
587 CHECK(args.IsConstructCall())do { if (__builtin_expect(!!(!(args.IsConstructCall())), 0)) {
do { static const node::AssertionInfo args = { "../src/node_file.cc"
":" "587", "args.IsConstructCall()", __PRETTY_FUNCTION__ }; node
::Assert(args); } while (0); } } while (0);
588 BindingData* binding_data = Environment::GetBindingData<BindingData>(args);
589 new FSReqCallback(binding_data, args.This(), args[0]->IsTrue());
590}

592FSReqAfterScope::FSReqAfterScope(FSReqBase* wrap, uv_fs_t* req)
593 : wrap_(wrap),
594 req_(req),
595 handle_scope_(wrap->env()->isolate()),
596 context_scope_(wrap->env()->context()) {
597 CHECK_EQ(wrap_->req(), req)do { if (__builtin_expect(!!(!((wrap_->req()) == (req))), 0
)) { do { static const node::AssertionInfo args = { "../src/node_file.cc"
":" "597", "(wrap_->req()) == (req)", __PRETTY_FUNCTION__
}; node::Assert(args); } while (0); } } while (0);
598}
599
600FSReqAfterScope::~FSReqAfterScope() {
601 Clear();
602}
603
604void FSReqAfterScope::Clear() {
605 if (!wrap_) return;
606
607 uv_fs_req_cleanup(wrap_->req());
608 wrap_->Detach();
609 wrap_.reset();
610}
611
612// TODO(joyeecheung): create a normal context object, and
613// construct the actual errors in the JS land using the context.
614// The context should include fds for some fs APIs, currently they are
615// missing in the error messages. The path, dest, syscall, fd, .etc
616// can be put into the context before the binding is even invoked,
617// the only information that has to come from the C++ layer is the
618// error number (and possibly the syscall for abstraction),
619// which is also why the errors should have been constructed
620// in JS for more flexibility.
621void FSReqAfterScope::Reject(uv_fs_t* req) {
622 BaseObjectPtr<FSReqBase> wrap { wrap_ };
623 Local<Value> exception =
624 UVException(wrap_->env()->isolate(),
625 req->result,
626 wrap_->syscall(),
627 nullptr,
628 req->path,
629 wrap_->data());
630 Clear();
631 wrap->Reject(exception);
632}
633
634bool FSReqAfterScope::Proceed() {
635 if (req_->result < 0) {
636 Reject(req_);
637 return false;
638 }
639 return true;
640}
641
642void AfterNoArgs(uv_fs_t* req) {
643 FSReqBase* req_wrap = FSReqBase::from_req(req);
644 FSReqAfterScope after(req_wrap, req);
645
646 if (after.Proceed())
647 req_wrap->Resolve(Undefined(req_wrap->env()->isolate()));
648}
649
650void AfterStat(uv_fs_t* req) {
651 FSReqBase* req_wrap = FSReqBase::from_req(req);
652 FSReqAfterScope after(req_wrap, req);
653
654 if (after.Proceed()) {
655 req_wrap->ResolveStat(&req->statbuf);
656 }
657}
658
659void AfterInteger(uv_fs_t* req) {
660 FSReqBase* req_wrap = FSReqBase::from_req(req);
661 FSReqAfterScope after(req_wrap, req);
662
663 if (req->result >= 0 && req_wrap->is_plain_open())
664 req_wrap->env()->AddUnmanagedFd(req->result);
665
666 if (after.Proceed())
667 req_wrap->Resolve(Integer::New(req_wrap->env()->isolate(), req->result));
668}
669
670void AfterOpenFileHandle(uv_fs_t* req) {
671 FSReqBase* req_wrap = FSReqBase::from_req(req);
672 FSReqAfterScope after(req_wrap, req);
673
674 if (after.Proceed()) {
675 FileHandle* fd = FileHandle::New(req_wrap->binding_data(), req->result);
676 if (fd == nullptr) return;
677 req_wrap->Resolve(fd->object());
678 }
679}
680
681// Reverse the logic applied by path.toNamespacedPath() to create a
682// namespace-prefixed path.
683void FromNamespacedPath(std::string* path) {
684#ifdef _WIN32
685 if (path->compare(0, 8, "\\\\?\\UNC\\", 8) == 0) {
686 *path = path->substr(8);
687 path->insert(0, "\\\\");
688 } else if (path->compare(0, 4, "\\\\?\\", 4) == 0) {
689 *path = path->substr(4);
690 }
691#endif
692}
693
694void AfterMkdirp(uv_fs_t* req) {
695 FSReqBase* req_wrap = FSReqBase::from_req(req);
696 FSReqAfterScope after(req_wrap, req);
697
698 MaybeLocal<Value> path;
699 Local<Value> error;
700
701 if (after.Proceed()) {
702 if (!req_wrap->continuation_data()->first_path().empty()) {
703 std::string first_path(req_wrap->continuation_data()->first_path());
704 FromNamespacedPath(&first_path);
705 path = StringBytes::Encode(req_wrap->env()->isolate(), first_path.c_str(),
706 req_wrap->encoding(),
707 &error);
708 if (path.IsEmpty())
709 req_wrap->Reject(error);
710 else
711 req_wrap->Resolve(path.ToLocalChecked());
712 } else {
713 req_wrap->Resolve(Undefined(req_wrap->env()->isolate()));
714 }
715 }
716}
717
718void AfterStringPath(uv_fs_t* req) {
719 FSReqBase* req_wrap = FSReqBase::from_req(req);
720 FSReqAfterScope after(req_wrap, req);
721
722 MaybeLocal<Value> link;
723 Local<Value> error;
724
725 if (after.Proceed()) {
726 link = StringBytes::Encode(req_wrap->env()->isolate(),
727 req->path,
728 req_wrap->encoding(),
729 &error);
730 if (link.IsEmpty())
731 req_wrap->Reject(error);
732 else
733 req_wrap->Resolve(link.ToLocalChecked());
734 }
735}
736
737void AfterStringPtr(uv_fs_t* req) {
738 FSReqBase* req_wrap = FSReqBase::from_req(req);
739 FSReqAfterScope after(req_wrap, req);
740
741 MaybeLocal<Value> link;
742 Local<Value> error;
743
744 if (after.Proceed()) {
745 link = StringBytes::Encode(req_wrap->env()->isolate(),
746 static_cast<const char*>(req->ptr),
747 req_wrap->encoding(),
748 &error);
749 if (link.IsEmpty())
750 req_wrap->Reject(error);
751 else
752 req_wrap->Resolve(link.ToLocalChecked());
753 }
754}
755
756void AfterScanDir(uv_fs_t* req) {
757 FSReqBase* req_wrap = FSReqBase::from_req(req);
758 FSReqAfterScope after(req_wrap, req);
759
760 if (!after.Proceed()) {
761 return;
762 }
763 Environment* env = req_wrap->env();
764 Local<Value> error;
765 int r;
766 std::vector<Local<Value>> name_v;
767
768 for (;;) {
769 uv_dirent_t ent;
770
771 r = uv_fs_scandir_next(req, &ent);
772 if (r == UV_EOF)
773 break;
774 if (r != 0) {
775 return req_wrap->Reject(UVException(
776 env->isolate(), r, nullptr, req_wrap->syscall(), req->path));
777 }
778
779 MaybeLocal<Value> filename =
780 StringBytes::Encode(env->isolate(),
781 ent.name,
782 req_wrap->encoding(),
783 &error);
784 if (filename.IsEmpty())
785 return req_wrap->Reject(error);
786
787 name_v.push_back(filename.ToLocalChecked());
788 }
789
790 req_wrap->Resolve(Array::New(env->isolate(), name_v.data(), name_v.size()));
791}
792
793void AfterScanDirWithTypes(uv_fs_t* req) {
794 FSReqBase* req_wrap = FSReqBase::from_req(req);
795 FSReqAfterScope after(req_wrap, req);
796
797 if (!after.Proceed()) {
798 return;
799 }
800
801 Environment* env = req_wrap->env();
802 Isolate* isolate = env->isolate();
803 Local<Value> error;
804 int r;
805
806 std::vector<Local<Value>> name_v;
807 std::vector<Local<Value>> type_v;
808
809 for (;;) {
810 uv_dirent_t ent;
811
812 r = uv_fs_scandir_next(req, &ent);
813 if (r == UV_EOF)
814 break;
815 if (r != 0) {
816 return req_wrap->Reject(
817 UVException(isolate, r, nullptr, req_wrap->syscall(), req->path));
818 }
819
820 MaybeLocal<Value> filename =
821 StringBytes::Encode(isolate,
822 ent.name,
823 req_wrap->encoding(),
824 &error);
825 if (filename.IsEmpty())
826 return req_wrap->Reject(error);
827
828 name_v.push_back(filename.ToLocalChecked());
829 type_v.emplace_back(Integer::New(isolate, ent.type));
830 }
831
832 Local<Value> result[] = {
833 Array::New(isolate, name_v.data(), name_v.size()),
834 Array::New(isolate, type_v.data(), type_v.size())
835 };
836 req_wrap->Resolve(Array::New(isolate, result, arraysize(result)));
837}

867void Close(const FunctionCallbackInfo<Value>& args) {
868 Environment* env = Environment::GetCurrent(args);
869
870 const int argc = args.Length();
871 CHECK_GE(argc, 2)do { if (__builtin_expect(!!(!((argc) >= (2))), 0)) { do {
static const node::AssertionInfo args = { "../src/node_file.cc"
":" "871", "(argc) >= (2)", __PRETTY_FUNCTION__ }; node::
Assert(args); } while (0); } } while (0);
872
873 CHECK(args[0]->IsInt32())do { if (__builtin_expect(!!(!(args[0]->IsInt32())), 0)) {
do { static const node::AssertionInfo args = { "../src/node_file.cc"
":" "873", "args[0]->IsInt32()", __PRETTY_FUNCTION__ }; node
::Assert(args); } while (0); } } while (0);
874 int fd = args[0].As<Int32>()->Value();
875 env->RemoveUnmanagedFd(fd);
876
877 FSReqBase* req_wrap_async = GetReqWrap(args, 1);
878 if (req_wrap_async != nullptr) { // close(fd, req)
879 AsyncCall(env, req_wrap_async, args, "close", UTF8, AfterNoArgs,
880 uv_fs_close, fd);
881 } else { // close(fd, undefined, ctx)
882 CHECK_EQ(argc, 3)do { if (__builtin_expect(!!(!((argc) == (3))), 0)) { do { static
const node::AssertionInfo args = { "../src/node_file.cc" ":"
"882", "(argc) == (3)", __PRETTY_FUNCTION__ }; node::Assert(
args); } while (0); } } while (0);
883 FSReqWrapSync req_wrap_sync;
884 FS_SYNC_TRACE_BEGIN(close)if ((*node::tracing::TraceEventHelper::GetCategoryGroupEnabled
("node" "," "node" "." "fs" "," "node" "." "fs" "." "sync") !=
0)) do { static std::atomic<intptr_t> trace_event_unique_atomic884
{0}; const uint8_t* trace_event_unique_category_group_enabled884
; trace_event_unique_category_group_enabled884 = reinterpret_cast
<const uint8_t*>((trace_event_unique_atomic884).load())
; if (!trace_event_unique_category_group_enabled884) { trace_event_unique_category_group_enabled884

890
891// Used to speed up module loading. Returns an array [string, boolean]
892static void InternalModuleReadJSON(const FunctionCallbackInfo<Value>& args) {
893 Environment* env = Environment::GetCurrent(args);
894 Isolate* isolate = env->isolate();
895 uv_loop_t* loop = env->event_loop();
896
897 CHECK(args[0]->IsString())do { if (__builtin_expect(!!(!(args[0]->IsString())), 0)) {
do { static const node::AssertionInfo args = { "../src/node_file.cc"
":" "897", "args[0]->IsString()", __PRETTY_FUNCTION__ }; node
::Assert(args); } while (0); } } while (0);
898 node::Utf8Value path(isolate, args[0]);
899
900 if (strlen(*path) != path.length()) {
901 args.GetReturnValue().Set(Array::New(isolate));
902 return; // Contains a nul byte.
903 }
904 uv_fs_t open_req;
905 const int fd = uv_fs_open(loop, &open_req, *path, O_RDONLY00, 0, nullptr);
906 uv_fs_req_cleanup(&open_req);
907
908 if (fd < 0) {
909 args.GetReturnValue().Set(Array::New(isolate));
910 return;
911 }
912
913 auto defer_close = OnScopeLeave([fd, loop]() {
914 uv_fs_t close_req;
915 CHECK_EQ(0, uv_fs_close(loop, &close_req, fd, nullptr))do { if (__builtin_expect(!!(!((0) == (uv_fs_close(loop, &
close_req, fd, nullptr)))), 0)) { do { static const node::AssertionInfo
args = { "../src/node_file.cc" ":" "915", "(0) == (uv_fs_close(loop, &close_req, fd, nullptr))"
, __PRETTY_FUNCTION__ }; node::Assert(args); } while (0); } }
while (0);
916 uv_fs_req_cleanup(&close_req);
917 });
918
919 const size_t kBlockSize = 32 << 10;
920 std::vector<char> chars;
921 int64_t offset = 0;
922 ssize_t numchars;
923 do {
924 const size_t start = chars.size();
925 chars.resize(start + kBlockSize);
926
927 uv_buf_t buf;
928 buf.base = &chars[start];
929 buf.len = kBlockSize;
930
931 uv_fs_t read_req;
932 numchars = uv_fs_read(loop, &read_req, fd, &buf, 1, offset, nullptr);
933 uv_fs_req_cleanup(&read_req);
934
935 if (numchars < 0) {
936 args.GetReturnValue().Set(Array::New(isolate));
937 return;
938 }
939 offset += numchars;
940 } while (static_cast<size_t>(numchars) == kBlockSize);
941
942 size_t start = 0;
943 if (offset >= 3 && 0 == memcmp(&chars[0], "\xEF\xBB\xBF", 3)) {
944 start = 3; // Skip UTF-8 BOM.
945 }
946
947 const size_t size = offset - start;
948 char* p = &chars[start];
949 char* pe = &chars[size];
950 char* pos[2];
951 char** ppos = &pos[0];
952
953 while (p < pe) {
954 char c = *p++;
955 if (c == '\\' && p < pe && *p == '"') p++;
956 if (c != '"') continue;
957 *ppos++ = p;
958 if (ppos < &pos[2]) continue;
959 ppos = &pos[0];
960
961 char* s = &pos[0][0];
962 char* se = &pos[1][-1]; // Exclude quote.
963 size_t n = se - s;
964
965 if (n == 4) {
966 if (0 == memcmp(s, "main", 4)) break;
967 if (0 == memcmp(s, "name", 4)) break;
968 if (0 == memcmp(s, "type", 4)) break;
969 } else if (n == 7) {
970 if (0 == memcmp(s, "exports", 7)) break;
971 if (0 == memcmp(s, "imports", 7)) break;
972 }
973 }
974
975
976 Local<Value> return_value[] = {
977 String::NewFromUtf8(isolate,
978 &chars[start],
979 v8::NewStringType::kNormal,
980 size).ToLocalChecked(),
981 Boolean::New(isolate, p < pe ? true : false)
982 };
983 args.GetReturnValue().Set(
984 Array::New(isolate, return_value, arraysize(return_value)));
985}
986
987// Used to speed up module loading. Returns 0 if the path refers to
988// a file, 1 when it's a directory or < 0 on error (usually -ENOENT.)
989// The speedup comes from not creating thousands of Stat and Error objects.
990static void InternalModuleStat(const FunctionCallbackInfo<Value>& args) {
991 Environment* env = Environment::GetCurrent(args);
992
993 CHECK(args[0]->IsString())do { if (__builtin_expect(!!(!(args[0]->IsString())), 0)) {
do { static const node::AssertionInfo args = { "../src/node_file.cc"
":" "993", "args[0]->IsString()", __PRETTY_FUNCTION__ }; node
::Assert(args); } while (0); } } while (0);
994 node::Utf8Value path(env->isolate(), args[0]);
995
996 uv_fs_t req;
997 int rc = uv_fs_stat(env->event_loop(), &req, *path, nullptr);
998 if (rc == 0) {
999 const uv_stat_t* const s = static_cast<const uv_stat_t*>(req.ptr);
1000 rc = !!(s->st_mode & S_IFDIR0040000);
1001 }
1002 uv_fs_req_cleanup(&req);
1003
1004 args.GetReturnValue().Set(rc);
1005}

1157static void ReadLink(const FunctionCallbackInfo<Value>& args) {

1194 }
1195
1196 args.GetReturnValue().Set(rc.ToLocalChecked());

1341
1342int MKDirpSync(uv_loop_t* loop,
1343 uv_fs_t* req,
1344 const std::string& path,
1345 int mode,
1346 uv_fs_cb cb) {
1347 FSReqWrapSync* req_wrap = ContainerOf(&FSReqWrapSync::req, req);
1348
1349 // on the first iteration of algorithm, stash state information.
1350 if (req_wrap->continuation_data() == nullptr) {
1351 req_wrap->set_continuation_data(
1352 std::make_unique<FSContinuationData>(req, mode, cb));
1353 req_wrap->continuation_data()->PushPath(std::move(path));
1354 }
1355
1356 while (req_wrap->continuation_data()->paths().size() > 0) {
1357 std::string next_path = req_wrap->continuation_data()->PopPath();
1358 int err = uv_fs_mkdir(loop, req, next_path.c_str(), mode, nullptr);
1359 while (true) {
1360 switch (err) {
1361 // Note: uv_fs_req_cleanup in terminal paths will be called by
1362 // ~FSReqWrapSync():
1363 case 0:
1364 req_wrap->continuation_data()->MaybeSetFirstPath(next_path);
1365 if (req_wrap->continuation_data()->paths().size() == 0) {
1366 return 0;
1367 }
1368 break;
1369 case UV_EACCES:
1370 case UV_ENOTDIR:
1371 case UV_EPERM: {
1372 return err;
1373 }
1374 case UV_ENOENT: {
1375 std::string dirname = next_path.substr(0,
1376 next_path.find_last_of(kPathSeparator));
1377 if (dirname != next_path) {
1378 req_wrap->continuation_data()->PushPath(std::move(next_path));
1379 req_wrap->continuation_data()->PushPath(std::move(dirname));
1380 } else if (req_wrap->continuation_data()->paths().size() == 0) {
1381 err = UV_EEXIST;
1382 continue;
1383 }
1384 break;
1385 }
1386 default:
1387 uv_fs_req_cleanup(req);
1388 int orig_err = err;
1389 err = uv_fs_stat(loop, req, next_path.c_str(), nullptr);
1390 if (err == 0 && !S_ISDIR(req->statbuf.st_mode)((((req->statbuf.st_mode)) & 0170000) == (0040000))) {
1391 uv_fs_req_cleanup(req);
1392 if (orig_err == UV_EEXIST &&
1393 req_wrap->continuation_data()->paths().size() > 0) {
1394 return UV_ENOTDIR;
1395 }
1396 return UV_EEXIST;
1397 }
1398 if (err < 0) return err;
1399 break;
1400 }
1401 break;
1402 }
1403 uv_fs_req_cleanup(req);
1404 }
1405
1406 return 0;
1407}
1408
1409int MKDirpAsync(uv_loop_t* loop,
1410 uv_fs_t* req,
1411 const char* path,
1412 int mode,
1413 uv_fs_cb cb) {
1414 FSReqBase* req_wrap = FSReqBase::from_req(req);
1415 // on the first iteration of algorithm, stash state information.
1416 if (req_wrap->continuation_data() == nullptr) {
1417 req_wrap->set_continuation_data(
1418 std::make_unique<FSContinuationData>(req, mode, cb));
1419 req_wrap->continuation_data()->PushPath(std::move(path));
1420 }
1421
1422 // on each iteration of algorithm, mkdir directory on top of stack.
1423 std::string next_path = req_wrap->continuation_data()->PopPath();
1424 int err = uv_fs_mkdir(loop, req, next_path.c_str(), mode,
1425 uv_fs_callback_t{[](uv_fs_t* req) {
1426 FSReqBase* req_wrap = FSReqBase::from_req(req);
1427 Environment* env = req_wrap->env();
1428 uv_loop_t* loop = env->event_loop();
1429 std::string path = req->path;
1430 int err = req->result;
1431
1432 while (true) {
1433 switch (err) {
1434 // Note: uv_fs_req_cleanup in terminal paths will be called by
1435 // FSReqAfterScope::~FSReqAfterScope()
1436 case 0: {
1437 if (req_wrap->continuation_data()->paths().size() == 0) {
1438 req_wrap->continuation_data()->MaybeSetFirstPath(path);
1439 req_wrap->continuation_data()->Done(0);
1440 } else {
1441 req_wrap->continuation_data()->MaybeSetFirstPath(path);
1442 uv_fs_req_cleanup(req);
1443 MKDirpAsync(loop, req, path.c_str(),
1444 req_wrap->continuation_data()->mode(), nullptr);
1445 }
1446 break;
1447 }
1448 case UV_EACCES:
1449 case UV_ENOTDIR:
1450 case UV_EPERM: {
1451 req_wrap->continuation_data()->Done(err);
1452 break;
1453 }
1454 case UV_ENOENT: {
1455 std::string dirname = path.substr(0,
1456 path.find_last_of(kPathSeparator));
1457 if (dirname != path) {
1458 req_wrap->continuation_data()->PushPath(std::move(path));
1459 req_wrap->continuation_data()->PushPath(std::move(dirname));
1460 } else if (req_wrap->continuation_data()->paths().size() == 0) {
1461 err = UV_EEXIST;
1462 continue;
1463 }
1464 uv_fs_req_cleanup(req);
1465 MKDirpAsync(loop, req, path.c_str(),
1466 req_wrap->continuation_data()->mode(), nullptr);
1467 break;
1468 }
1469 default:
1470 uv_fs_req_cleanup(req);
1471 // Stash err for use in the callback.
1472 req->data = reinterpret_cast<void*>(static_cast<intptr_t>(err));
1473 int err = uv_fs_stat(loop, req, path.c_str(),
1474 uv_fs_callback_t{[](uv_fs_t* req) {
1475 FSReqBase* req_wrap = FSReqBase::from_req(req);
1476 int err = req->result;
1477 if (reinterpret_cast<intptr_t>(req->data) == UV_EEXIST &&
1478 req_wrap->continuation_data()->paths().size() > 0) {
1479 if (err == 0 && S_ISDIR(req->statbuf.st_mode)((((req->statbuf.st_mode)) & 0170000) == (0040000))) {
1480 Environment* env = req_wrap->env();
1481 uv_loop_t* loop = env->event_loop();
1482 std::string path = req->path;
1483 uv_fs_req_cleanup(req);
1484 MKDirpAsync(loop, req, path.c_str(),
1485 req_wrap->continuation_data()->mode(), nullptr);
1486 return;
1487 }
1488 err = UV_ENOTDIR;
1489 }
1490 // verify that the path pointed to is actually a directory.
1491 if (err == 0 && !S_ISDIR(req->statbuf.st_mode)((((req->statbuf.st_mode)) & 0170000) == (0040000))) err = UV_EEXIST;
1492 req_wrap->continuation_data()->Done(err);
1493 }});
1494 if (err < 0) req_wrap->continuation_data()->Done(err);
1495 break;
1496 }
1497 break;
1498 }
1499 }});
1500
1501 return err;
1502}
1503
1504int CallMKDirpSync(Environment* env, const FunctionCallbackInfo<Value>& args,
1505 FSReqWrapSync* req_wrap, const char* path, int mode) {
1506 env->PrintSyncTrace();
1507 int err = MKDirpSync(env->event_loop(), &req_wrap->req, path, mode,
1508 nullptr);
1509 if (err < 0) {
1510 v8::Local<v8::Context> context = env->context();
1511 v8::Local<v8::Object> ctx_obj = args[4].As<v8::Object>();
1512 v8::Isolate* isolate = env->isolate();
1513 ctx_obj->Set(context,
1514 env->errno_string(),
1515 v8::Integer::New(isolate, err)).Check();
1516 ctx_obj->Set(context,
1517 env->syscall_string(),
1518 OneByteString(isolate, "mkdir")).Check();
1519 }
1520 return err;
1521}

1571
1572static void RealPath(const FunctionCallbackInfo<Value>& args) {
1573 Environment* env = Environment::GetCurrent(args);
1574 Isolate* isolate = env->isolate();
1575
1576 const int argc = args.Length();
1577 CHECK_GE(argc, 3)do { if (__builtin_expect(!!(!((argc) >= (3))), 0)) { do {
static const node::AssertionInfo args = { "../src/node_file.cc"
":" "1577", "(argc) >= (3)", __PRETTY_FUNCTION__ }; node::
Assert(args); } while (0); } } while (0);
1578
1579 BufferValue path(isolate, args[0]);
1580 CHECK_NOT_NULL(*path)do { if (__builtin_expect(!!(!((*path) != nullptr)), 0)) { do
{ static const node::AssertionInfo args = { "../src/node_file.cc"
":" "1580", "(*path) != nullptr", __PRETTY_FUNCTION__ }; node
::Assert(args); } while (0); } } while (0);
1581
1582 const enum encoding encoding = ParseEncoding(isolate, args[1], UTF8);
1583

1616static void ReadDir(const FunctionCallbackInfo<Value>& args) {
1617 Environment* env = Environment::GetCurrent(args);
1618 Isolate* isolate = env->isolate();
1619
1620 const int argc = args.Length();
1621 CHECK_GE(argc, 3)do { if (__builtin_expect(!!(!((argc) >= (3))), 0)) { do {

":" "1621", "(argc) >= (3)", __PRETTY_FUNCTION__ }; node::
Assert(args); } while (0); } } while (0);

::Assert(args); } while (0); } } while (0);
1625

1627

1629
1630 FSReqBase* req_wrap_async = GetReqWrap(args, 3);
1631 if (req_wrap_async != nullptr) { // readdir(path, encoding, withTypes, req)
1632 if (with_types) {
1633 AsyncCall(env, req_wrap_async, args, "scandir", encoding,
1634 AfterScanDirWithTypes, uv_fs_scandir, *path, 0 /*flags*/);
1635 } else {
1636 AsyncCall(env, req_wrap_async, args, "scandir", encoding,
1637 AfterScanDir, uv_fs_scandir, *path, 0 /*flags*/);
1638 }
1639 } else { // readdir(path, encoding, withTypes, undefined, ctx)
1640 CHECK_EQ(argc, 5)do { if (__builtin_expect(!!(!((argc) == (5))), 0)) { do { static
const node::AssertionInfo args = { "../src/node_file.cc" ":"
"1640", "(argc) == (5)", __PRETTY_FUNCTION__ }; node::Assert
(args); } while (0); } } while (0);
1641 FSReqWrapSync req_wrap_sync;
1642 FS_SYNC_TRACE_BEGIN(readdir)if ((*node::tracing::TraceEventHelper::GetCategoryGroupEnabled
("node" "," "node" "." "fs" "," "node" "." "fs" "." "sync") !=
0)) do { static std::atomic<intptr_t> trace_event_unique_atomic1642
{0}; const uint8_t* trace_event_unique_category_group_enabled1642
; trace_event_unique_category_group_enabled1642 = reinterpret_cast
<const uint8_t*>((trace_event_unique_atomic1642).load()
); if (!trace_event_unique_category_group_enabled1642) { trace_event_unique_category_group_enabled1642
= node::tracing::TraceEventHelper::GetCategoryGroupEnabled("node"
"," "node" "." "fs" "," "node" "." "fs" "." "sync"); (trace_event_unique_atomic1642
).store(reinterpret_cast<intptr_t>( trace_event_unique_category_group_enabled1642
)); };; if (*trace_event_unique_category_group_enabled1642 &

)) { node::tracing::AddTraceEvent( ('B'), trace_event_unique_category_group_enabled1642
, "fs.sync." "readdir", node::tracing::kGlobalScope, node::tracing
::kNoId, node::tracing::kNoId, (static_cast<unsigned int>
(0))); } } while (0);;
1643 int err = SyncCall(env, args[4], &req_wrap_sync, "scandir",
1644 uv_fs_scandir, *path, 0 /*flags*/);
1645 FS_SYNC_TRACE_END(readdir)if ((*node::tracing::TraceEventHelper::GetCategoryGroupEnabled
("node" "," "node" "." "fs" "," "node" "." "fs" "." "sync") !=
0)) do { static std::atomic<intptr_t> trace_event_unique_atomic1645
{0}; const uint8_t* trace_event_unique_category_group_enabled1645
; trace_event_unique_category_group_enabled1645 = reinterpret_cast
<const uint8_t*>((trace_event_unique_atomic1645).load()
); if (!trace_event_unique_category_group_enabled1645) { trace_event_unique_category_group_enabled1645
= node::tracing::TraceEventHelper::GetCategoryGroupEnabled("node"
"," "node" "." "fs" "," "node" "." "fs" "." "sync"); (trace_event_unique_atomic1645
).store(reinterpret_cast<intptr_t>( trace_event_unique_category_group_enabled1645
)); };; if (*trace_event_unique_category_group_enabled1645 &
(kEnabledForRecording_CategoryGroupEnabledFlags | kEnabledForEventCallback_CategoryGroupEnabledFlags
)) { node::tracing::AddTraceEvent( ('E'), trace_event_unique_category_group_enabled1645
, "fs.sync." "readdir", node::tracing::kGlobalScope, node::tracing
::kNoId, node::tracing::kNoId, (static_cast<unsigned int>
(0))); } } while (0);;
1646 if (err < 0) {
1647 return; // syscall failed, no need to continue, error info is in ctx
1648 }
1649
1650 CHECK_GE(req_wrap_sync.req.result, 0)do { if (__builtin_expect(!!(!((req_wrap_sync.req.result) >=
(0))), 0)) { do { static const node::AssertionInfo args = { "../src/node_file.cc"
":" "1650", "(req_wrap_sync.req.result) >= (0)", __PRETTY_FUNCTION__
}; node::Assert(args); } while (0); } } while (0);
1651 int r;
1652 std::vector<Local<Value>> name_v;
1653 std::vector<Local<Value>> type_v;
1654
1655 for (;;) {
1656 uv_dirent_t ent;
1657
1658 r = uv_fs_scandir_next(&(req_wrap_sync.req), &ent);
1659 if (r == UV_EOF)
1660 break;
1661 if (r != 0) {
1662 Local<Object> ctx = args[4].As<Object>();
1663 ctx->Set(env->context(), env->errno_string(),
1664 Integer::New(isolate, r)).Check();
1665 ctx->Set(env->context(), env->syscall_string(),
1666 OneByteString(isolate, "readdir")).Check();
1667 return;
1668 }
1669
1670 Local<Value> error;
1671 MaybeLocal<Value> filename = StringBytes::Encode(isolate,
1672 ent.name,
1673 encoding,
1674 &error);
1675
1676 if (filename.IsEmpty()) {
1677 Local<Object> ctx = args[4].As<Object>();
1678 ctx->Set(env->context(), env->error_string(), error).Check();
1679 return;
1680 }
1681
1682 name_v.push_back(filename.ToLocalChecked());
1683
1684 if (with_types) {
1685 type_v.emplace_back(Integer::New(isolate, ent.type));
1686 }
1687 }
1688
1689
1690 Local<Array> names = Array::New(isolate, name_v.data(), name_v.size());
1691 if (with_types) {
1692 Local<Value> result[] = {
1693 names,
1694 Array::New(isolate, type_v.data(), type_v.size())
1695 };
1696 args.GetReturnValue().Set(Array::New(isolate, result, arraysize(result)));
1697 } else {
1698 args.GetReturnValue().Set(names);
1699 }
1700 }
1701}

1905// Wrapper for write(2).
1906//
1907// bytesWritten = write(fd, string, position, enc, callback)
1908// 0 fd integer. file descriptor
1909// 1 string non-buffer values are converted to strings
1910// 2 position if integer, position to write at in the file.
1911// if null, write from the current position
1912// 3 enc encoding of string
1913static void WriteString(const FunctionCallbackInfo<Value>& args) {
1914 Environment* env = Environment::GetCurrent(args);
1915 Isolate* isolate = env->isolate();
1916
1917 const int argc = args.Length();
1918 CHECK_GE(argc, 4)do { if (__builtin_expect(!!(!((argc) >= (4))), 0)) { do {
static const node::AssertionInfo args = { "../src/node_file.cc"
":" "1918", "(argc) >= (4)", __PRETTY_FUNCTION__ }; node::
Assert(args); } while (0); } } while (0);
1919
1920 CHECK(args[0]->IsInt32())do { if (__builtin_expect(!!(!(args[0]->IsInt32())), 0)) {
do { static const node::AssertionInfo args = { "../src/node_file.cc"
":" "1920", "args[0]->IsInt32()", __PRETTY_FUNCTION__ }; node
::Assert(args); } while (0); } } while (0);
1921 const int fd = args[0].As<Int32>()->Value();
1922
1923 const int64_t pos = GetOffset(args[2]);
1924
1925 const auto enc = ParseEncoding(isolate, args[3], UTF8);
1926
1927 Local<Value> value = args[1];
1928 char* buf = nullptr;
1929 size_t len;
1930
1931 FSReqBase* req_wrap_async = GetReqWrap(args, 4);
1932 const bool is_async = req_wrap_async != nullptr;
1933
1934 // Avoid copying the string when it is externalized but only when:
1935 // 1. The target encoding is compatible with the string's encoding, and
1936 // 2. The write is synchronous, otherwise the string might get neutered
1937 // while the request is in flight, and
1938 // 3. For UCS2, when the host system is little-endian. Big-endian systems
1939 // need to call StringBytes::Write() to ensure proper byte swapping.
1940 // The const_casts are conceptually sound: memory is read but not written.
1941 if (!is_async && value->IsString()) {
1942 auto string = value.As<String>();
1943 if ((enc == ASCII || enc == LATIN1) && string->IsExternalOneByte()) {
1944 auto ext = string->GetExternalOneByteStringResource();
1945 buf = const_cast<char*>(ext->data());
1946 len = ext->length();
1947 } else if (enc == UCS2 && IsLittleEndian() && string->IsExternalTwoByte()) {
1948 auto ext = string->GetExternalStringResource();
1949 buf = reinterpret_cast<char*>(const_cast<uint16_t*>(ext->data()));
1950 len = ext->length() * sizeof(*ext->data());
1951 }
1952 }
1953
1954 if (is_async) { // write(fd, string, pos, enc, req)
1955 CHECK_NOT_NULL(req_wrap_async)do { if (__builtin_expect(!!(!((req_wrap_async) != nullptr)),
0)) { do { static const node::AssertionInfo args = { "../src/node_file.cc"
":" "1955", "(req_wrap_async) != nullptr", __PRETTY_FUNCTION__
}; node::Assert(args); } while (0); } } while (0);
1956 if (!StringBytes::StorageSize(isolate, value, enc).To(&len)) return;
1957 FSReqBase::FSReqBuffer& stack_buffer =
1958 req_wrap_async->Init("write", len, enc);
1959 // StorageSize may return too large a char, so correct the actual length
1960 // by the write size
1961 len = StringBytes::Write(isolate, *stack_buffer, len, args[1], enc);
1962 stack_buffer.SetLengthAndZeroTerminate(len);
1963 uv_buf_t uvbuf = uv_buf_init(*stack_buffer, len);
1964 int err = req_wrap_async->Dispatch(uv_fs_write,
1965 fd,
1966 &uvbuf,
1967 1,
1968 pos,
1969 AfterInteger);
1970 if (err < 0) {
1971 uv_fs_t* uv_req = req_wrap_async->req();
1972 uv_req->result = err;
1973 uv_req->path = nullptr;
1974 AfterInteger(uv_req); // after may delete req_wrap_async if there is
1975 // an error
1976 } else {
1977 req_wrap_async->SetReturnValue(args);
1978 }
1979 } else { // write(fd, string, pos, enc, undefined, ctx)
1980 CHECK_EQ(argc, 6)do { if (__builtin_expect(!!(!((argc) == (6))), 0)) { do { static
const node::AssertionInfo args = { "../src/node_file.cc" ":"
"1980", "(argc) == (6)", __PRETTY_FUNCTION__ }; node::Assert
(args); } while (0); } } while (0);
1981 FSReqWrapSync req_wrap_sync;
1982 FSReqBase::FSReqBuffer stack_buffer;
1983 if (buf == nullptr) {
1984 if (!StringBytes::StorageSize(isolate, value, enc).To(&len))
1985 return;
1986 stack_buffer.AllocateSufficientStorage(len + 1);
1987 // StorageSize may return too large a char, so correct the actual length
1988 // by the write size
1989 len = StringBytes::Write(isolate, *stack_buffer,
1990 len, args[1], enc);
1991 stack_buffer.SetLengthAndZeroTerminate(len);
1992 buf = *stack_buffer;
1993 }
1994 uv_buf_t uvbuf = uv_buf_init(buf, len);
1995 FS_SYNC_TRACE_BEGIN(write)if ((*node::tracing::TraceEventHelper::GetCategoryGroupEnabled
("node" "," "node" "." "fs" "," "node" "." "fs" "." "sync") !=
0)) do { static std::atomic<intptr_t> trace_event_unique_atomic1995
{0}; const uint8_t* trace_event_unique_category_group_enabled1995
; trace_event_unique_category_group_enabled1995 = reinterpret_cast
<const uint8_t*>((trace_event_unique_atomic1995).load()
); if (!trace_event_unique_category_group_enabled1995) { trace_event_unique_category_group_enabled1995
= node::tracing::TraceEventHelper::GetCategoryGroupEnabled("node"
"," "node" "." "fs" "," "node" "." "fs" "." "sync"); (trace_event_unique_atomic1995
).store(reinterpret_cast<intptr_t>( trace_event_unique_category_group_enabled1995
)); };; if (*trace_event_unique_category_group_enabled1995 &
(kEnabledForRecording_CategoryGroupEnabledFlags | kEnabledForEventCallback_CategoryGroupEnabledFlags
)) { node::tracing::AddTraceEvent( ('B'), trace_event_unique_category_group_enabled1995
, "fs.sync." "write", node::tracing::kGlobalScope, node::tracing
::kNoId, node::tracing::kNoId, (static_cast<unsigned int>
(0))); } } while (0);;
1996 int bytesWritten = SyncCall(env, args[5], &req_wrap_sync, "write",
1997 uv_fs_write, fd, &uvbuf, 1, pos);
1998 FS_SYNC_TRACE_END(write, "bytesWritten", bytesWritten)if ((*node::tracing::TraceEventHelper::GetCategoryGroupEnabled
("node" "," "node" "." "fs" "," "node" "." "fs" "." "sync") !=
0)) do { static std::atomic<intptr_t> trace_event_unique_atomic1998
{0}; const uint8_t* trace_event_unique_category_group_enabled1998
; trace_event_unique_category_group_enabled1998 = reinterpret_cast
<const uint8_t*>((trace_event_unique_atomic1998).load()
); if (!trace_event_unique_category_group_enabled1998) { trace_event_unique_category_group_enabled1998
= node::tracing::TraceEventHelper::GetCategoryGroupEnabled("node"
"," "node" "." "fs" "," "node" "." "fs" "." "sync"); (trace_event_unique_atomic1998
).store(reinterpret_cast<intptr_t>( trace_event_unique_category_group_enabled1998
)); };; if (*trace_event_unique_category_group_enabled1998 &
(kEnabledForRecording_CategoryGroupEnabledFlags | kEnabledForEventCallback_CategoryGroupEnabledFlags
)) { node::tracing::AddTraceEvent( ('E'), trace_event_unique_category_group_enabled1998
, "fs.sync." "write", node::tracing::kGlobalScope, node::tracing
::kNoId, node::tracing::kNoId, (static_cast<unsigned int>
(0)), "bytesWritten", bytesWritten); } } while (0);;
1999 args.GetReturnValue().Set(bytesWritten);
2000 }
2001}

2004/*
2005 * Wrapper for read(2).
2006 *
2007 * bytesRead = fs.read(fd, buffer, offset, length, position)
2008 *
2009 * 0 fd int32. file descriptor
2010 * 1 buffer instance of Buffer
2011 * 2 offset int64. offset to start reading into inside buffer

111inline void AsyncHooks::push_async_context(double async_id,
112 double trigger_async_id,
113 v8::Local<v8::Object> resource) {

}; node::Assert(args); } while (0); } } while (0);

125 async_ids_stack_[2 * offset + 1] = async_id_fields_[kTriggerAsyncId];

145// Remember to keep this code aligned with popAsyncContext() in JS.
146inline bool AsyncHooks::pop_async_context(double async_id) {
147 // In case of an exception then this may have already been reset, if the
148 // stack was multiple MakeCallback()'s deep.
149 if (fields_[kStackLength] == 0) return false;
150
151 // Ask for the async_id to be restored as a check that the stack
152 // hasn't been corrupted.
153 // Since async_hooks is experimental, do only perform the check
154 // when async_hooks is enabled.
155 if (fields_[kCheck] > 0 && async_id_fields_[kExecutionAsyncId] != async_id) {
156 fprintf(stderrstderr,
157 "Error: async hook stack has become corrupted ("
158 "actual: %.f, expected: %.f)\n",
159 async_id_fields_.GetValue(kExecutionAsyncId),
160 async_id);
161 DumpBacktrace(stderrstderr);
162 fflush(stderrstderr);
163 if (!env()->abort_on_uncaught_exception())
164 exit(1);
165 fprintf(stderrstderr, "\n");
166 fflush(stderrstderr);
167 ABORT_NO_BACKTRACE()abort();
168 }
169
170 uint32_t offset = fields_[kStackLength] - 1;
171 async_id_fields_[kExecutionAsyncId] = async_ids_stack_[2 * offset];
172 async_id_fields_[kTriggerAsyncId] = async_ids_stack_[2 * offset + 1];
173 fields_[kStackLength] = offset;
174
175 if (LIKELY(offset < native_execution_async_resources_.size() &&__builtin_expect(!!(offset < native_execution_async_resources_
.size() && !native_execution_async_resources_[offset]
.IsEmpty()), 1)
176 !native_execution_async_resources_[offset].IsEmpty())__builtin_expect(!!(offset < native_execution_async_resources_
.size() && !native_execution_async_resources_[offset]
.IsEmpty()), 1)) {
177#ifdef DEBUG
178 for (uint32_t i = offset + 1;
179 i < native_execution_async_resources_.size();
180 i++) {
181 CHECK(native_execution_async_resources_[i].IsEmpty())do { if (__builtin_expect(!!(!(native_execution_async_resources_
[i].IsEmpty())), 0)) { do { static const node::AssertionInfo args
= { "../src/env-inl.h" ":" "181", "native_execution_async_resources_[i].IsEmpty()"
, __PRETTY_FUNCTION__ }; node::Assert(args); } while (0); } }
while (0);
182 }
183#endif
184 native_execution_async_resources_.resize(offset);
185 if (native_execution_async_resources_.size() <
186 native_execution_async_resources_.capacity() / 2 &&
187 native_execution_async_resources_.size() > 16) {
188 native_execution_async_resources_.shrink_to_fit();
189 }
190 }
191
192 if (UNLIKELY(js_execution_async_resources()->Length() > offset)__builtin_expect(!!(js_execution_async_resources()->Length
() > offset), 0)) {
193 v8::HandleScope handle_scope(env()->isolate());
194 USE(js_execution_async_resources()->Set(
195 env()->context(),
196 env()->length_string(),
197 v8::Integer::NewFromUnsigned(env()->isolate(), offset)));
198 }
199
200 return fields_[kStackLength] > 0;
201}
202
203void AsyncHooks::clear_async_id_stack() {
204 v8::Isolate* isolate = env()->isolate();
205 v8::HandleScope handle_scope(isolate);
206 if (!js_execution_async_resources_.IsEmpty()) {
207 USE(PersistentToLocal::Strong(js_execution_async_resources_)->Set(
208 env()->context(),
209 env()->length_string(),
210 v8::Integer::NewFromUnsigned(isolate, 0)));
211 }
212 native_execution_async_resources_.clear();
213 native_execution_async_resources_.shrink_to_fit();
214
215 async_id_fields_[kExecutionAsyncId] = 0;
216 async_id_fields_[kTriggerAsyncId] = 0;
217 fields_[kStackLength] = 0;
218}

293inline void Environment::AssignToContext(v8::Local<v8::Context> context,
294 const ContextInfo& info) {
295 context->SetAlignedPointerInEmbedderData(
296 ContextEmbedderIndex::kEnvironment, this);
297 // Used by Environment::GetCurrent to know that we are on a node context.
298 context->SetAlignedPointerInEmbedderData(
299 ContextEmbedderIndex::kContextTag, Environment::kNodeContextTagPtr);
300 // Used to retrieve bindings
301 context->SetAlignedPointerInEmbedderData(
302 ContextEmbedderIndex::kBindingListIndex, &(this->bindings_));
303
304#if HAVE_INSPECTOR1
305 inspector_agent()->ContextCreated(context, info);
306#endif // HAVE_INSPECTOR
307}

355template <typename T>
356inline T* Environment::GetBindingData(v8::Local<v8::Context> context) {
357 BindingDataStore* map = static_cast<BindingDataStore*>(
358 context->GetAlignedPointerFromEmbedderData(
359 ContextEmbedderIndex::kBindingListIndex));
360 DCHECK_NOT_NULL(map);
361 auto it = map->find(T::binding_data_name);
362 if (UNLIKELY(it == map->end())__builtin_expect(!!(it == map->end()), 0)) return nullptr;
363 T* result = static_cast<T*>(it->second.get());
364 DCHECK_NOT_NULL(result);
365 DCHECK_EQ(result->env(), GetCurrent(context));
366 return result;
367}

417template <typename T, typename OnCloseCallback>
418inline void Environment::CloseHandle(T* handle, OnCloseCallback callback) {
419 handle_cleanup_waiting_++;
420 static_assert(sizeof(T) >= sizeof(uv_handle_t), "T is a libuv handle");
421 static_assert(offsetof(T, data)__builtin_offsetof(T, data) == offsetof(uv_handle_t, data)__builtin_offsetof(uv_handle_t, data),
422 "T is a libuv handle");
423 static_assert(offsetof(T, close_cb)__builtin_offsetof(T, close_cb) == offsetof(uv_handle_t, close_cb)__builtin_offsetof(uv_handle_t, close_cb),
424 "T is a libuv handle");
425 struct CloseData {
426 Environment* env;
427 OnCloseCallback callback;
428 void* original_data;
429 };
430 handle->data = new CloseData { this, callback, handle->data };
431 uv_close(reinterpret_cast<uv_handle_t*>(handle), [](uv_handle_t* handle) {
432 std::unique_ptr<CloseData> data { static_cast<CloseData*>(handle->data) };
433 data->env->handle_cleanup_waiting_--;
434 handle->data = data->original_data;
435 data->callback(reinterpret_cast<T*>(handle));
436 });
437}

613inline std::string Environment::GetCwd() {
614 char cwd[PATH_MAX_BYTES(4096)];
615 size_t size = PATH_MAX_BYTES(4096);
616 const int err = uv_cwd(cwd, &size);
617
618 if (err == 0) {
619 CHECK_GT(size, 0)do { if (__builtin_expect(!!(!((size) > (0))), 0)) { do { static
const node::AssertionInfo args = { "../src/env-inl.h" ":" "619"
, "(size) > (0)", __PRETTY_FUNCTION__ }; node::Assert(args
); } while (0); } } while (0);
620 return cwd;
621 }
622
623 // This can fail if the cwd is deleted. In that case, fall back to
624 // exec_path.
625 const std::string& exec_path = exec_path_;
626 return exec_path.substr(0, exec_path.find_last_of(kPathSeparator));
627}

734template <typename Fn>
735void Environment::SetImmediate(Fn&& cb, CallbackFlags::Flags flags) {
736 auto callback = native_immediates_.CreateCallback(std::move(cb), flags);
737 native_immediates_.Push(std::move(callback));
738
739 if (flags & CallbackFlags::kRefed) {
740 if (immediate_info()->ref_count() == 0)
741 ToggleImmediateRef(true);
742 immediate_info()->ref_count_inc(1);
743 }
744}
745
746template <typename Fn>
747void Environment::SetImmediateThreadsafe(Fn&& cb, CallbackFlags::Flags flags) {
748 auto callback = native_immediates_threadsafe_.CreateCallback(
749 std::move(cb), flags);
750 {
751 Mutex::ScopedLock lock(native_immediates_threadsafe_mutex_);
752 native_immediates_threadsafe_.Push(std::move(callback));
753 if (task_queues_async_initialized_)
754 uv_async_send(&task_queues_async_);
755 }
756}
757
758template <typename Fn>
759void Environment::RequestInterrupt(Fn&& cb) {
760 auto callback = native_immediates_interrupts_.CreateCallback(
761 std::move(cb), CallbackFlags::kRefed);
762 {
763 Mutex::ScopedLock lock(native_immediates_threadsafe_mutex_);
764 native_immediates_interrupts_.Push(std::move(callback));
765 if (task_queues_async_initialized_)
766 uv_async_send(&task_queues_async_);
767 }
768 RequestInterruptFromV8();
769}

919inline void Environment::ThrowErrnoException(int errorno,

922 const char* path) {
923 isolate()->ThrowException(
924 ErrnoException(isolate(), errorno, syscall, message, path));
925}
926
927inline void Environment::ThrowUVException(int errorno,
928 const char* syscall,
929 const char* message,
930 const char* path,
931 const char* dest) {
932 isolate()->ThrowException(
933 UVException(isolate(), errorno, syscall, message, path, dest));
934}
935
936inline v8::Local<v8::FunctionTemplate>
937 Environment::NewFunctionTemplate(v8::FunctionCallback callback,
938 v8::Local<v8::Signature> signature,
939 v8::ConstructorBehavior behavior,
940 v8::SideEffectType side_effect_type) {
941 return v8::FunctionTemplate::New(isolate(), callback, v8::Local<v8::Value>(),
942 signature, 0, behavior, side_effect_type);
943}
944
945inline void Environment::SetMethod(v8::Local<v8::Object> that,
946 const char* name,
947 v8::FunctionCallback callback) {
948 v8::Local<v8::Context> context = isolate()->GetCurrentContext();
949 v8::Local<v8::Function> function =
950 NewFunctionTemplate(callback, v8::Local<v8::Signature>(),
951 v8::ConstructorBehavior::kThrow,
952 v8::SideEffectType::kHasSideEffect)
953 ->GetFunction(context)
954 .ToLocalChecked();
955 // kInternalized strings are created in the old space.
956 const v8::NewStringType type = v8::NewStringType::kInternalized;
957 v8::Local<v8::String> name_string =
958 v8::String::NewFromUtf8(isolate(), name, type).ToLocalChecked();
959 that->Set(context, name_string, function).Check();
960 function->SetName(name_string); // NODE_SET_METHOD() compatibility.
961}
962
963inline void Environment::SetMethodNoSideEffect(v8::Local<v8::Object> that,
964 const char* name,
965 v8::FunctionCallback callback) {
966 v8::Local<v8::Context> context = isolate()->GetCurrentContext();
967 v8::Local<v8::Function> function =
968 NewFunctionTemplate(callback, v8::Local<v8::Signature>(),
969 v8::ConstructorBehavior::kThrow,
970 v8::SideEffectType::kHasNoSideEffect)
971 ->GetFunction(context)
972 .ToLocalChecked();
973 // kInternalized strings are created in the old space.
974 const v8::NewStringType type = v8::NewStringType::kInternalized;
975 v8::Local<v8::String> name_string =
976 v8::String::NewFromUtf8(isolate(), name, type).ToLocalChecked();
977 that->Set(context, name_string, function).Check();
978 function->SetName(name_string); // NODE_SET_METHOD() compatibility.
979}
980
981inline void Environment::SetProtoMethod(v8::Local<v8::FunctionTemplate> that,
982 const char* name,
983 v8::FunctionCallback callback) {
984 v8::Local<v8::Signature> signature = v8::Signature::New(isolate(), that);
985 v8::Local<v8::FunctionTemplate> t =
986 NewFunctionTemplate(callback, signature, v8::ConstructorBehavior::kThrow,
987 v8::SideEffectType::kHasSideEffect);
988 // kInternalized strings are created in the old space.
989 const v8::NewStringType type = v8::NewStringType::kInternalized;
990 v8::Local<v8::String> name_string =
991 v8::String::NewFromUtf8(isolate(), name, type).ToLocalChecked();
992 that->PrototypeTemplate()->Set(name_string, t);
993 t->SetClassName(name_string); // NODE_SET_PROTOTYPE_METHOD() compatibility.
994}
995

997 v8::Local<v8::FunctionTemplate> that,

1010}

1012inline void Environment::SetInstanceMethod(v8::Local<v8::FunctionTemplate> that,
1013 const char* name,
1014 v8::FunctionCallback callback) {
1015 v8::Local<v8::Signature> signature = v8::Signature::New(isolate(), that);

1026
1027void Environment::AddCleanupHook(void (*fn)(void*), void* arg) {
1028 auto insertion_info = cleanup_hooks_.emplace(CleanupHookCallback {
1029 fn, arg, cleanup_hook_counter_++
1030 });
1031 // Make sure there was no existing element with these values.
1032 CHECK_EQ(insertion_info.second, true)do { if (__builtin_expect(!!(!((insertion_info.second) == (true
))), 0)) { do { static const node::AssertionInfo args = { "../src/env-inl.h"
":" "1032", "(insertion_info.second) == (true)", __PRETTY_FUNCTION__
}; node::Assert(args); } while (0); } } while (0);
1033}
1034
1035void Environment::RemoveCleanupHook(void (*fn)(void*), void* arg) {
1036 CleanupHookCallback search { fn, arg, 0 };
1037 cleanup_hooks_.erase(search);
1038}
1039
1040size_t CleanupHookCallback::Hash::operator()(
1041 const CleanupHookCallback& cb) const {
1042 return std::hash<void*>()(cb.arg_);
1043}
1044
1045bool CleanupHookCallback::Equal::operator()(
1046 const CleanupHookCallback& a, const CleanupHookCallback& b) const {
1047 return a.fn_ == b.fn_ && a.arg_ == b.arg_;
1048}
1049
1050BaseObject* CleanupHookCallback::GetBaseObject() const {
1051 if (fn_ == BaseObject::DeleteMe)
1052 return static_cast<BaseObject*>(arg_);
1053 else
1054 return nullptr;
1055}
1056
1057template <typename T>
1058void Environment::ForEachBaseObject(T&& iterator) {
1059 for (const auto& hook : cleanup_hooks_) {
1060 BaseObject* obj = hook.GetBaseObject();
1061 if (obj != nullptr)
1062 iterator(obj);
1063 }
1064}
1065
1066void Environment::modify_base_object_count(int64_t delta) {
1067 base_object_count_ += delta;
1068}
1069
1070int64_t Environment::base_object_count() const {
1071 return base_object_count_ - initial_base_object_count_;
1072}
1073
1074void Environment::set_main_utf16(std::unique_ptr<v8::String::Value> str) {
1075 CHECK(!main_utf16_)do { if (__builtin_expect(!!(!(!main_utf16_)), 0)) { do { static
const node::AssertionInfo args = { "../src/env-inl.h" ":" "1075"
, "!main_utf16_", __PRETTY_FUNCTION__ }; node::Assert(args); }
while (0); } } while (0);
1076 main_utf16_ = std::move(str);
1077}
1078
1079void Environment::set_process_exit_handler(
1080 std::function<void(Environment*, int)>&& handler) {
1081 process_exit_handler_ = std::move(handler);
1082}

96BaseObject* BaseObject::FromJSObject(v8::Local<v8::Value> value) {

110void BaseObject::MakeWeak() {

135void BaseObject::ClearWeak() {

142bool BaseObject::IsWeakOrDetached() const {
143 if (persistent_handle_.IsWeak()) return true;
144
145 if (!has_pointer_data()) return false;
146 const PointerData* pd = const_cast<BaseObject*>(this)->pointer_data();
147 return pd->wants_weak_jsobj || pd->is_detached;
148}

150v8::Local<v8::FunctionTemplate>
151BaseObject::MakeLazilyInitializedJSTemplate(Environment* env) {
152 auto constructor = [](const v8::FunctionCallbackInfo<v8::Value>& args) {
153 DCHECK(args.IsConstructCall());
154 DCHECK_GT(args.This()->InternalFieldCount(), 0);
155 args.This()->SetAlignedPointerInInternalField(BaseObject::kSlot, nullptr);
156 };
157
158 v8::Local<v8::FunctionTemplate> t = env->NewFunctionTemplate(constructor);
159 t->Inherit(BaseObject::GetConstructorTemplate(env));
160 t->InstanceTemplate()->SetInternalFieldCount(
161 BaseObject::kInternalFieldCount);
162 return t;
163}

210void BaseObject::increase_refcount() {
211 unsigned int prev_refcount = pointer_data()->strong_ptr_count++;

265 } else {
266 data_.target = target;
267 CHECK_NOT_NULL(pointer_data())do { if (__builtin_expect(!!(!((pointer_data()) != nullptr)),
0)) { do { static const node::AssertionInfo args = { "../src/base_object-inl.h"
":" "267", "(pointer_data()) != nullptr", __PRETTY_FUNCTION__
}; node::Assert(args); } while (0); } } while (0);
268 get()->increase_refcount();
269 }
270}
271
272template <typename T, bool kIsWeak>
273template <typename U, bool kW>
274BaseObjectPtrImpl<T, kIsWeak>::BaseObjectPtrImpl(
275 const BaseObjectPtrImpl<U, kW>& other)
276 : BaseObjectPtrImpl(other.get()) {}
277
278template <typename T, bool kIsWeak>
279BaseObjectPtrImpl<T, kIsWeak>::BaseObjectPtrImpl(const BaseObjectPtrImpl& other)
280 : BaseObjectPtrImpl(other.get()) {}
281
282template <typename T, bool kIsWeak>
283template <typename U, bool kW>
284BaseObjectPtrImpl<T, kIsWeak>& BaseObjectPtrImpl<T, kIsWeak>::operator=(
285 const BaseObjectPtrImpl<U, kW>& other) {
286 if (other.get() == get()) return *this;
287 this->~BaseObjectPtrImpl();
288 return *new (this) BaseObjectPtrImpl(other);
289}
290
291template <typename T, bool kIsWeak>
292BaseObjectPtrImpl<T, kIsWeak>& BaseObjectPtrImpl<T, kIsWeak>::operator=(
293 const BaseObjectPtrImpl& other) {
294 if (other.get() == get()) return *this;
295 this->~BaseObjectPtrImpl();
296 return *new (this) BaseObjectPtrImpl(other);
297}
298
299template <typename T, bool kIsWeak>
300BaseObjectPtrImpl<T, kIsWeak>::BaseObjectPtrImpl(BaseObjectPtrImpl&& other)
301 : data_(other.data_) {
302 if (kIsWeak)
303 other.data_.target = nullptr;
304 else
305 other.data_.pointer_data = nullptr;
306}
307
308template <typename T, bool kIsWeak>
309BaseObjectPtrImpl<T, kIsWeak>& BaseObjectPtrImpl<T, kIsWeak>::operator=(
310 BaseObjectPtrImpl&& other) {
311 if (&other == this) return *this;
312 this->~BaseObjectPtrImpl();
313 return *new (this) BaseObjectPtrImpl(std::move(other));
314}
315
316template <typename T, bool kIsWeak>
317void BaseObjectPtrImpl<T, kIsWeak>::reset(T* ptr) {
318 *this = BaseObjectPtrImpl(ptr);
319}
320
321template <typename T, bool kIsWeak>
322T* BaseObjectPtrImpl<T, kIsWeak>::get() const {
323 return static_cast<T*>(get_base_object());
324}
325
326template <typename T, bool kIsWeak>
327T& BaseObjectPtrImpl<T, kIsWeak>::operator*() const {
328 return *get();
329}
330
331template <typename T, bool kIsWeak>
332T* BaseObjectPtrImpl<T, kIsWeak>::operator->() const {
333 return get();
334}
335
336template <typename T, bool kIsWeak>
337BaseObjectPtrImpl<T, kIsWeak>::operator bool() const {
338 return get() != nullptr;
339}
340
341template <typename T, bool kIsWeak>
342template <typename U, bool kW>
343bool BaseObjectPtrImpl<T, kIsWeak>::operator ==(
344 const BaseObjectPtrImpl<U, kW>& other) const {
345 return get() == other.get();
346}
347
348template <typename T, bool kIsWeak>
349template <typename U, bool kW>
350bool BaseObjectPtrImpl<T, kIsWeak>::operator !=(
351 const BaseObjectPtrImpl<U, kW>& other) const {
352 return get() != other.get();
353}
354
355template <typename T, typename... Args>
356BaseObjectPtr<T> MakeBaseObject(Args&&... args) {
357 return BaseObjectPtr<T>(new T(std::forward<Args>(args)...));
358}
359
360template <typename T, typename... Args>
361BaseObjectPtr<T> MakeDetachedBaseObject(Args&&... args) {
362 BaseObjectPtr<T> target = MakeBaseObject<T>(std::forward<Args>(args)...);
363 target->Detach();
364 return target;
365}
